> **2026-04-25 — ORCH-0676 FORENSICS RETURNED + REVIEW APPROVED → STEERING DECISION REQUIRED. CYCLE-1 ORCH-0675 RC-9 FRAMING REVERSED.** Audit: [reports/INVESTIGATION_ORCH-0676_DECK_DELIVERY_AUDIT.md](Mingla_Artifacts/reports/INVESTIGATION_ORCH-0676_DECK_DELIVERY_AUDIT.md). **Three cycle-1 framings overturned by direct-file verification:** (1) `limit: 10000` is THEATRE — discover-cards line 888 hardcodes `perChipRpcLimit = max(20, min(100, limit*2))` so actual server cap is **100 per chip**; production deck size ~300-700 cards (5 chips), NOT 10,000. (2) `excludeCardIds` is wired through edge fn + RPC (`p_exclude_place_ids`) but **all 5 production callers pass `[]`** (RecommendationsContext.tsx:629/656/685/739, OnboardingFlow.tsx:1643/1657) — server-side dedup is functionally DEAD. (3) `batchSeed` looks like pagination handle but discover-cards reads it (lines 629/753/1021) and **never consumes it** — incrementing it changes React Query cache key, forces refetch, server returns SAME cards in SAME order. **CRITICAL DISCOVERY (D-1, S0 pre-existing defect):** the founder's non-negotiable invariant ("user can exhaust every scored card in a session") **IS ALREADY BROKEN IN PRODUCTION** for any user whose pool exceeds first-batch size (~300-700 cards). The pagination handle exists in code but the server has NO offset/cursor parameter — there is no path to additional cards beyond the first batch today. SwipeableCards.tsx:1050 increments batchSeed, refetch fires, server returns same cards, client `removedCards` filter excludes already-swiped, `availableRecommendations` stays empty, user sees empty state despite scored cards existing. **This pre-existing defect was MASKED by cycle-1 RC-9's misframing.** Capping deck or removing-from-persister WITHOUT first fixing pagination would have AMPLIFIED this regression. Founder pushback was correct. **3 client persistence substrates documented:** (a) React Query persister deck-cards key; (b) Zustand `sessionSwipedCards` storing FULL Recommendation objects ~200×~2KB=~400KB persisted (vs ~10KB ID-only manifest = 40× waste); (c) SwipeableCards' own `mingla_card_state_${mode}_${refreshKey}_*` AsyncStorage keys (the actual production dedup filter). 1.5MB cache cap is nuke-from-orbit (Constitution #14 violation). **5 ranked efficiency options A-E + 2 supplementary F/G** each with full regression-risk matrix across 10-12 dimensions. **Solo/collab parity:** ORCH-0446 collab uses same `useDeckCards` with mode='collab' + sessionId discriminant; cross-user dedup is INTENTIONALLY OFF per ORCH-0446 design. **Recommended direction (NOT a spec):** bundle Options A+B+C+D as ONE coordinated SPEC. Option A (real cursor pagination — `(p_after_score numeric, p_after_id uuid)` on RPCs + edge fn forwarding + client cursor-trigger when ~10 cards remain + first-page-only persistence) is the ONLY option that resolves D-1 pre-existing exhaustion defect. Option B (populate `excludeCardIds` from solo `removedCards` Set — skip in collab to preserve ORCH-0446) becomes mandatory under pagination. Option C (Zustand sessionSwipedCardIds as `string[]` instead of full Recommendation[]) saves ~98% Zustand persist cost. Option D (per-key AsyncStorage cap instead of nuke-from-orbit) closes Constitution #14. Option E DEFERRED to Wave 2.B. Option F DEFERRED to Wave 3. **5 new invariant candidates:** I-DECK-PAGINATION-WORKS, I-DECK-DEDUP-EXPLICIT, I-ZUSTAND-CARD-IDS-ONLY, I-PERSISTER-PER-KEY-CAP, I-DECK-EXHAUSTION-CONTRACT. **6 discoveries:** D-1 EXHAUSTION INVARIANT ALREADY BROKEN (S0 pre-existing — most consequential); D-2 sub-agent claims verified by direct read on consequential ones; D-3 5 invariant candidates queued; D-4 Constitution #5 at-risk by design; D-5 empty-state UX path NOT audited (Q-20); D-6 production analytics gap. **REVIEW (10 gates PASS):** root causes proven via direct-file verification; scope tight; hidden fallbacks documented (stale-prune, 1.5s dead-state recovery); stale cache paths exhaustively mapped; response-shape gap (empty-state UX) flagged INSUFFICIENT-EVIDENCE not hidden; INVESTIGATE-ONLY honored (only direction recommended); solo/collab parity audited explicitly; Constitutional violations mapped #2/#5/#14; evidence chain complete with 9 prioritized live-fire gaps. **Founder steering Q-13 through Q-20 open in §8.** Orchestrator defaults: Q-13 bundle A+B+C+D in one SPEC; Q-14 page size 70; Q-15 cursor-based pagination (stable under concurrent writes); Q-16 first-page-only persistence; Q-17 use SwipeableCards `removedCards` (mode/refreshKey-scoped) for `excludeCardIds`; Q-18 collab cross-user dedup remains OFF (preserve ORCH-0446); Q-19 reset cursor on day rollover; Q-20 include empty-state UX in SPEC scope. **WAVE 1 (ORCH-0675 RC-1+2+3+Zustand-debounce, no deck touch) STILL VIABLE IN PARALLEL** — narrow blast radii, OTA-eligible. **Two SPEC dispatches once founder confirms steering:** Wave 1 (4 items) + Wave 2 (Options A+B+C+D + empty-state UX). > **2026-04-25 — ORCH-0668 FORENSICS RETURNED HIGH + REVIEW APPROVED → SPEC DISPATCH READY.** Investigation: `reports/INVESTIGATION_ORCH-0668_PAIRED_PROFILE_RECOMMENDATIONS_FAIL.md`. **Root cause PROVEN HIGH:** `query_person_hero_places_by_signal` is `LANGUAGE plpgsql VOLATILE`. After ≥5 invocations per session, plpgsql plan caching switches to a generic plan that picks a poor join order, materializes huge intermediate sets, spills to temp files, and exceeds the 8-second `statement_timeout` on the `authenticator` role (inherited by service_role since its rolconfig is NULL). Edge fn returns 500 `"Database query failed"` after ~8s; mobile React Query enters `isError`; every `<CardRow>` renders the offline error state. **Live-fire matrix:** identical inner CTE inline = **87 ms**, wrapped in plpgsql RPC = **8169 ms** (6 signals) / **25 206 ms** (11 signals). Edge function logs: 8 sequential 500s clustered at 8.4-8.7 s — exact PostgREST kill timing. `pg_get_functiondef` confirms deployed body matches migration `20260425000007` source verbatim (no drift; the bug IS the language choice). Sibling RPCs `query_servable_places_by_signal` (singles deck) and `fetch_local_signal_ranked` (curated post-ORCH-0653) are `LANGUAGE sql STABLE` and run <300ms — language asymmetry is the smoking gun. **Findings:** 1 RC + 2 CF + 4 HF + 2 OBS. **Constitutional violations:** #3 (silent failure — generic 500 hides timeout vs error), #8 (subtract before add — WHILE LOOP dead weight, never iterates at urban locations because 1797 places ≥ 9 limit at Raleigh's 15km band). **New invariant registered:** `I-RPC-LANGUAGE-SQL-FOR-HOT-PATH` — any user-facing hot-path RPC with array/composite parameters must be `LANGUAGE sql STABLE`, or `LANGUAGE plpgsql` with explicit `SET plan_cache_mode = force_custom_plan` + documented justification. **Blast radius:** single surface (paired-profile recommendations); singles deck + curated unaffected. **6 discoveries:** D-1 audit other plpgsql RPCs with array params (P3 separate dispatch), D-2 timeout-vs-error mobile UI (bundled HF-1), D-3 service_role.statement_timeout explicit (P4 separate), D-4 cron MV refresh 79s (P4 separate), D-5 WHILE LOOP elimination (bundled HF-3), D-6 no degraded-mode fallback (P3 separate). **REVIEW (orchestrator, 10 gates PASS):** RC proven via 5-layer reconcile + live-fire; scope tight; HF-1 + HF-3 bundled; no stale cache; subtract-before-add honored; solo/collab parity not violated (language-not-mode asymmetry); evidence chain complete. **SPEC dispatch:** `prompts/SPEC_ORCH-0668_PAIRED_PROFILE_RPC_FIX.md` — single migration (rewrite RPC as `LANGUAGE sql STABLE`, eliminate WHILE LOOP via fixed-band CTE, preserve signature + 3 gates), edge fn HF-1 response shape (503 timeout vs 500 error) + duration logging, CI gate registering `I-RPC-LANGUAGE-SQL-FOR-HOT-PATH`, ≤2s p95 perf budget at 11-signal Raleigh, 15 success criteria, 15 test cases, rollback plan, zero mobile changes. **Recommended Option A** (LANGUAGE sql STABLE) over Option B (plpgsql + plan_cache_mode) — 87ms inline plan probe is the proof. Constitutional #1 dead-tap-equivalent (tap appears responsive but produces wrong destination). **(F-2, S1)** receiver does NOT see pending pill — root cause `boardSessionService.ts:181-199` `fetchUserBoardSessions` collapses every non-completed/non-archived database status (including `'pending'`) → `boardStatus = 'active'` via the else-fallthrough at L198. Receiver's pending session arrives at `boardsSessions` with `status: 'active'` instead of `'pending'`; memo at `app/index.tsx:662` checks `if (board.status === 'pending')` — never true for receiver path → type stays `'active'` → renders as active orange-glow pill OR (if `pending_friendship: true` blocks `pendingInvitedSessions` for non-friend invitees) vanishes entirely. Sender path was protected by dedup-pending-first against the same misclassification — receiver path has no equivalent protection. **Investigation discovery ORCH-0661.D-1 (parallel session-state authorities) is now load-bearing**, not a deferred concern. **Cycle-2 implementor dispatch written:** `prompts/IMPL_ORCH-0661_REWORK_v2.md` covering both fixes — F-1 single-line guard at `HomePage.tsx` (skip `onSessionSelect(id)` for pending pills), F-2 schema preservation in `boardSessionService.ts` (extend `boardStatus` union to include `'pending'` AND remove the else-fallthrough collapse, OR add `dbStatus` passthrough field — implementor chooses cleanest). Tester re-dispatch after rework. **Retest cycle 2 of 2** — last rework before architect escalation. User action: dispatch `/mingla-implementor` against the rework prompt.

> **2026-04-25 — ORCH-0653 v3.1 deployed v141 (commit `7737119a`) — chunking didn't fully fix it. New failure: Supabase edge proxy `error sending request` even at 500-ID chunks (~20KB URL).** (SUPERSEDED by v3.2 CLOSED above.) All 6 intents at Raleigh return HTTP 500 on chunk 1/5. Different error than v3's Deno `Invalid URL`. The Supabase/Cloudflare edge proxy has a smaller URL cap than Deno fetch (~10-12KB vs ~64KB). To stay under that cap we'd need ~200-ID chunks → 25 sequential roundtrips per intent → ~2s overhead. **Pivoting to architectural fix: RPC push-down.** Write a Postgres RPC `fetch_local_signal_ranked(filter_signal, filter_min, rank_signal, lat_min, lat_max, lng_min, lng_max, required_types, limit)` that does the entire bbox+filter+rank query server-side in ONE call, returns top-N place_ids + scores. No `.in()` over thousands of IDs — IN happens inside Postgres where no URL constraint exists. Total roundtrips: 2 (RPC + Step 3 hydrate) instead of 5-15 chunked. v3.2 = 1 new migration + ~20 LOC code refactor. Pure architectural improvement — also fastest design. Recovery bundle AH-170: 0641 ✅, 0643 ✅ scoring, **0653 v3.2 RPC dispatch pending**, 0644 ⏳, 0642 ⏳.

TypeError: Invalid URL` — Step 0 returned 2106 bbox candidates for nature + casual_food, and the resulting `.in('place_id', bboxIds)` URL exceeded Deno fetch's ~64KB URL length cap. v1's Constitution #3 throws correctly surfaced the error (NOT silent — system worked as designed). 2/4 errored on `Unknown experienceType: date-night` / `brunch-explorer` (orchestrator passed wrong intent IDs in matrix; actual IDs are adventurous, first-date, romantic, group-fun, picnic-dates, take-a-stroll — re-run matrix with correct names). **v3.1 fix needed:** chunk the `.in()` calls into batches of ~500 IDs in Step 1 (and Step 2 if eligibleIds also exceeds limit). > **2026-04-24 night — ORCH-0653 v3 ROOT CAUSE PROVEN (HIGH confidence) — system-wide architectural bug.** v2 instrumentation deployed v139 (commit `fcce2ccc`). Live-fire revealed killer gate: `gate-reverseAnchor_no_available iter=7 catId=groceries anchor.gpid=ChIJL7C1g7TwrIkRj8ymStBSWYI categoryPlaces[nearKey].length=0`. Anchor identified as William B. Umstead State Park (lat 35.8894, lng -78.7518, 16km NW of Raleigh center). Direct MCP probes: 22 grocery candidates EXIST in DB within 3km bbox of Umstead, but `fetchSinglesForSignalRank` returns 0. **Root cause: Step 2 ranks GLOBALLY (top 60 by score across entire DB), then Step 3 applies user bbox filter.** Top 60 globally for groceries = 7 in Raleigh (city center, far from Umstead) + 1 in Fort Lauderdale + 52 in London (Iceland Supermarket / Sainsbury's chains dominate global scoring). Zero of those 60 fall within 3km of Umstead → Step 3 returns []. **Blast radius: every curated experience type in every city outside London since ORCH-0640 demolition.** Standard (non-anchor) flow scrapes by for Raleigh because 7 of top-60 happen to be in Raleigh's 17.5km bbox; tight-radius near-anchor calls (3km picnic) get zero. The pre-existing card_pool path (deleted by ORCH-0640) had per-city pre-filtering that masked this bug. **Fix architecture:** swap operation order — apply geographic bbox FIRST (Step 0 fetches local place_pool ids), then signal threshold filter (Step 1), then rank within local set (Step 2), then hydrate (Step 3). Ensures top N is always N local survivors. Single-file, single-function refactor in `supabase/functions/generate-curated-experiences/index.ts:310-456`. v3 dispatch prompt next.

> **ORCH-0540 (NEW 2026-04-19 15:32 UTC — P0 REGRESSION, rules-engine RPCs broken):** Every non-overview rules-engine RPC (`admin_rules_list`, `admin_rule_detail`, `admin_rule_set_versions`, `admin_rule_set_diff`, `admin_rules_preview_impact`, `admin_rules_runs`, `admin_rules_run_detail`, `admin_rules_run_diff`, `admin_rules_export`, `admin_rules_run_affected_places`) fails with `ERROR 42883: function row_to_jsonb(record) does not exist`. **Discovered immediately post-flip** when user opened admin Rules Filter tab: manifest label loaded (admin_rules_overview works — uses jsonb_build_object), but rule list and run history both errored with the same message. **Root cause verified via MCP DO $$ ... $$ block** at 2026-04-19 15:32 UTC: PL/pgSQL cannot resolve `row_to_jsonb(t)` when `t` is a subquery alias — Postgres sees generic `record` type and finds no overload match. **Fix (mechanical, 16 substitutions in 10 function definitions):** swap `row_to_jsonb(t)` → `to_jsonb(t)` everywhere in `supabase/migrations/20260420000003_create_rules_engine_rpcs.sql`. `to_jsonb` is polymorphic (`anyelement`) and handles subquery-aliased records cleanly. **Flag already reverted to `false` at 15:32 UTC.** Hotfix via new migration `20260420000005_fix_rules_rpcs_to_jsonb.sql` with CREATE OR REPLACE on 10 functions + user runs `supabase db push` + user re-flips flag + user browser spot-checks. Classification: bug + regression + data-integrity (user-visible broken UI in production). Severity: **P0 (critical)** — rules engine UI is unusable until fixed. **LESSON LOGGED (in QA report v2 pending):** "headless tester code-forensic PASS is insufficient when RPCs have never been called through the actual UI path. raw SQL that reproduces the subquery body ≠ running the RPC in plpgsql context. Future admin-UI QA dispatches must include 'dev-flag-flip + admin-UI-live-fire' as a mandatory pre-CLOSE gate." — Going into feedback memory.

> **ORCH-0539 (NEW 2026-04-19 15:29 UTC — P3 security-hygiene, non-blocking):** `admin_get_feature_flags(TEXT[])` SECURITY DEFINER function was GRANTed EXECUTE to `authenticated` but PUBLIC default EXECUTE was not REVOKEd. Both `anon` and `authenticated` roles have EXECUTE privilege. **No actual vulnerability today** — the function's internal `admin_users WHERE email = lower(auth.email()) AND status = 'active'` gate fails for anon callers (NULL auth.email() → EXISTS check returns false → RAISE EXCEPTION). Defense-in-depth suggests narrower surface. **Fix (single-line migration):** `REVOKE EXECUTE ON FUNCTION public.admin_get_feature_flags(TEXT[]) FROM PUBLIC;`. Bundle into future admin RPC hardening pass. Discovered during ORCH-0526 M4.2 tester MCP probe. Classification: security + architecture-flaw. S3 (low priority). Not bundled with ORCH-0526 CLOSE because charter is already shipped + Grade A; tracking independently for future cleanup.

Lesson logged: "hypothesis that fits existing data without live-reproduction proof is MEDIUM confidence, not HIGH." | Original: **ORCH-0532 INVESTIGATION AMENDED 2026-04-19 evening (HIGH-initially, downgraded MEDIUM on user challenge):** User device-tested the bug and reported "I swiped a card and it went directly to the session cards tab" — falsifying the original RC-1 (which pointed at tap-save paths in expanded modal / dismissed sheet). Investigator rescanned per Forensic Thoroughness Rules, found the real mechanism, and amended the report. **Corrected RC-1': Dual-source divergence.** Two components check "am I in a session?" from DIFFERENT state sources. (a) `SwipeableCards.isBoardSession` depends on `resolvedSessionId` which is derived from `availableSessions` coming from the `useSessionManagement()` hook (network-backed, lags on cold-launch / just-created session / just-accepted invite) — see [SwipeableCards.tsx:550-570](app-mobile/src/components/SwipeableCards.tsx#L550-L570). (b) `AppHandlers.handleSaveCard.isInSession` reads `stateRef.current.boardsSessions` from the Zustand global store (updates immediately via `setBoardsSessions`) — see [AppHandlers.tsx:681-694](app-mobile/src/components/AppHandlers.tsx#L681-L694). When (a) lags while (b) is fresh: `isBoardSession = false` so the primary swipe gesture takes the solo branch at [SwipeableCards.tsx:1499](app-mobile/src/components/SwipeableCards.tsx#L1499) → calls `onCardLike(card)` → `handleSaveCard` sees session via (b) → direct `INSERT INTO board_saved_cards` via `BoardCardService.saveCardToBoard` (bypasses `check_mutual_like` trigger which only fires on `board_user_swipe_states` writes). Simultaneously `trackSwipeState` at [:1538](app-mobile/src/components/SwipeableCards.tsx#L1538) is skipped (also gated by `isBoardSession`). Net: saved-card row exists, ZERO swipe-state rows. **DB proof:** session `3f1fa200` has 1 `board_saved_cards` row for user `c727d491` on Assaggio's (2026-04-19 05:41:59) and 0 `board_user_swipe_states` rows from that user in that session. That pattern is mechanically impossible under any other code path. Also confirmed: `check_mutual_like_trigger` is correctly installed (was not the culprit); `bsc_insert` RLS allows user-context direct inserts (defense-in-depth gap = ORCH-0535); 6 total anomaly rows in production data. **Original RC-1 demoted to CF-0** (real co-existing leak — 3 unguarded `onCardLike` callsites at SwipeableCards.tsx:1633, :1885, :2417 — still needs closing). **Option D recommended fix:** make `handleSaveCard` solo-only (remove collab branch lines 766-874), unify "am I in a session?" source of truth, route all collab saves exclusively through `BoardCardService.trackSwipeState` → trigger. This single change eliminates BOTH RC-1' AND CF-0 structurally. **2 new invariants:** I-SESSION-STATE-SINGLE-SOURCE, I-HANDLE-SAVE-CARD-IS-SOLO-ONLY. Classification: bug + invariant-violation + data-integrity + architecture-flaw (dual-source-of-truth). Severity: S1. Constitutional #2 violation ("One owner per truth"). **Process note:** investigator's original HIGH-confidence finding was wrong. Rescan on user challenge recovered. Lesson logged in report §16.8: "when two functions gate on 'same' state, verify they read from the same source, not just that both have a check." Report: `outputs/INVESTIGATION_ORCH-0532_COLLAB_SWIPE_TO_BOARD.md`. **SPEC prompt PENDING** — awaiting user steering on 2 open questions (see ORCH-0532 entry in Priority Board). Counter: +2 (ORCH-0535 + 0536 registered as side discoveries; 0533/0534 pre-registered).

> **ORCH-0533 (side discovery from ORCH-0532, S2 missing-feature):** Curated cards in collab sessions generate ZERO `board_user_swipe_states` rows. The curated-card branch at [SwipeableCards.tsx:1443-1461](app-mobile/src/components/SwipeableCards.tsx#L1443-L1461) correctly skips `onCardLike` in collab mode, but the shared `trackSwipeState` block at line 1538 is inside the `else` of `if (cardType === 'curated')`, so curated cards never fall through. Net: curated experiences can NEVER match in collab (no quorum can ever be reached). Recommend bundling into ORCH-0532 spec (same file, same mental model, zero extra test cost).

> **ORCH-0534 (side discovery from ORCH-0532, S3 data-integrity):** 4 historical `board_saved_cards` rows (2026-04-02) pre-date the mutual-like trigger (2026-04-11) and have `right_swiper_count = 0`. These are pre-existing anomaly artifacts from the old direct-save behavior. Product decision needed: leave as-is (sessions may already be consumed by users) or backfill/clean. Defer until product triages.

> **ORCH-0535 (side discovery from ORCH-0532, S2 security / architecture-flaw):** `bsc_insert` RLS policy at [20250227000005_fix_all_session_rls_and_triggers.sql:209-213](supabase/migrations/20250227000005_fix_all_session_rls_and_triggers.sql#L209-L213) allows any session participant to INSERT into `board_saved_cards` with only `saved_by = auth.uid() AND is_session_participant`. NO quorum check at RLS layer. Even after the ORCH-0532 client fix, a malicious or bugged client could still bypass quorum. Defense-in-depth: tighten RLS so only the `check_mutual_like` trigger (SECURITY DEFINER context) can insert. Recommend bundling into ORCH-0532 spec as defensive hardening.

> **ORCH-0536 (side discovery from ORCH-0532, S3 architecture-flaw — RESOLVED BY ORCH-0532 FIX):** `AppHandlers.handleSaveCard` is dual-mode (solo → `saved_card` table, collab → `board_saved_cards`). This design is the proximate vulnerability enabling RC-1' and CF-0. Option D in the ORCH-0532 fix removes the collab branch entirely, making `handleSaveCard` solo-only. ORCH-0536 is therefore resolved administratively by the ORCH-0532 implementation. Closing as "bundled — no separate work needed".

> **ORCH-0526 (Rules Engine) Phase 4 M2 SMOKE TEST PARTIAL FAIL 2026-04-19 (initial):** Deployed edge fn v33 + smoke tested on Fort Lauderdale (2,247 places, completed in 40s). 4 of 5 bundled bug fixes PASS via MCP verification: ✅ stage='rules_only_complete' (ORCH-0512), ✅ unchanged=1905 + approved=0 (ORCH-0527), ✅ city_id populated (ORCH-0530), ✅ lock_token populated (ORCH-0529). **❌ ORCH-0526 core path FAILED:** `rules_version_id = NULL` on the job + all 342 result rows have `rule_set_version_id = NULL`. Reasons match in-code constant strings exactly → `loadRulesFromDb` returned null and the I-RULES-FALLBACK-SAFE transition guard engaged. Diagnosis (orchestrator MCP probes): SQL-level JOIN works (18 versions × 18 rule_sets joined cleanly) — root cause is PostgREST FK auto-detection cache; the `rule_sets!inner(...)` embedded-resource syntax in loadRulesFromDb requires PostgREST to recognize the FK from rule_set_versions.rule_set_id → rule_sets.id. Sent `NOTIFY pgrst, 'reload schema'` (Path A). Path A failed (see entry above) → Path B dispatched.

> **ORCH-0533 (NEW 2026-04-19 — stale-run cleanup gap, S3):** Discovered by ORCH-0526 M2 implementor. If a rules-only run via `handleRunRulesFilter` crashes mid-execution, it stays `status='running'` forever and blocks all future runs on the same city via the new ORCH-0529 concurrency check. `handleRunBatch` (AI runs) has 5-minute stale-batch cleanup (lines 1070-1081) but `handleRunRulesFilter` doesn't have an analogous mechanism. Manual mitigation today: `UPDATE ai_validation_jobs SET status='cancelled' WHERE id='...'`. Fix: add same 5-minute stale-detection at handler entry (~5 lines). Not blocking — rules-only runs typically complete in seconds; crash is rare. S3 process-debt. Address in v2 of ORCH-0526 OR standalone.

> **ORCH-0532 (NEW 2026-04-19 — collab quorum invariant violation, S1):** User in a 2-person collaboration session reports a **single right-swipe lands the card immediately on the session's Cards tab**, instead of waiting for ≥2 participants to right-swipe the same card. Breaks the fundamental collab contract ("a card only becomes a match when multiple participants agree"). Preliminary evidence from orchestrator intake: the server-side `check_mutual_like` trigger at [20260411500001_mutual_like_trigger.sql:50](supabase/migrations/20260411500001_mutual_like_trigger.sql#L50) correctly enforces `v_right_swipe_count < 2 → RETURN NEW` — so the bug is almost certainly client-side and falls into one of: (A) a parallel write path inserting into `board_saved_cards` directly, (B) the Cards tab reading from a source OTHER than `board_saved_cards` (e.g., own `board_user_swipe_states` right-swipes), (C) a React Query optimistic update populating a session-matches cache without server confirmation, (D) realtime broadcast handler misinterpreting own `card_swipe` events as matches, (E) `savedCardsService` being invoked in collab mode as if solo, (F) a legacy trigger bypassing the 2+ check, or (G) trigger not actually installed in the user's live DB. Classification: bug + invariant-violation + data-integrity + regression-candidate. Severity S1 — breaks core collab value prop even though no crash. User directive: the fix must also correctly handle 3+ participant sessions with mixed save/pass. Invariants at stake: I-MATCH-REQUIRES-QUORUM, I-NO-SOLO-MATCH-IN-COLLAB, I-CARDS-TAB-SINGLE-SOURCE, I-OPTIMISTIC-WRITE-RESPECTS-QUORUM, I-SWIPE-WRITE-SINGLE-PATH. Forensics prompt: `prompts/FORENSICS_ORCH-0532_COLLAB_SWIPE_TO_BOARD_BUG.md` — scoped to investigate-only (no code, no spec, HIGH-confidence required). Report target: `outputs/INVESTIGATION_ORCH-0532_COLLAB_SWIPE_TO_BOARD.md`. **Awaiting user dispatch to mingla-forensics.**

> **ORCH-0531 (NEW 2026-04-19 evening — known limitation, deferred):** Rule rollback (admin_rules_rollback RPC) creates a new rule_set_version matching the target version, but does NOT auto-restore prior AI verdicts on places affected by the rolled-back rule. Concrete scenario: AI accepts Bar Vento → rules-v8 rejects Bar Vento (overwrites place_pool.ai_approved=false) → admin rolls back to v7 → re-runs rules-filter → rules don't fire on Bar Vento (no rule rejects it) → place_pool.ai_approved STAYS at false (last-writer-wins). Bar Vento doesn't reappear in decks. v1 mitigations: (a) history preserved in ai_validation_results so admin can SEE the AI verdict that got overwritten, (b) admin can manually override via Review Queue (existing admin_ai_override_place RPC), (c) re-running AI validation on affected places restores verdicts (costs OpenAI tokens), (d) impact preview before save (spec §5.2) makes the bad-rule-save scenario rare. v2 fix options: snapshot last_ai_verdict on place_pool OR compute on-the-fly from ai_validation_results history. ~2-3 days build. Classification: missing-feature + ux. S3 (low — has manual mitigation, low frequency expected). Discovered via user product question on ORCH-0526 Phase 3 spec review.

> **ORCH-0527 (NEW 2026-04-19 — misleading admin label, S2):** `ai_validation_jobs.approved` field for rules-only runs is misnamed — it's computed as `total_processed - rejected - reclassified` at edge function line 1606, which means the count of UNCHANGED places, not newly-approved places. Admin "Recent Runs" displays "approved=1212" which an admin reads as "1212 places approved by this run" but actually means "1212 places left alone by this run." Constitutional #3 adjacent (misleading rather than silent). Fix: rename to `unchanged` for rules-only runs OR add separate counters. Bundle with ORCH-0526 Phase 3 spec.

> **ORCH-0528 (NEW 2026-04-19 — silent drift, S2):** Four separate sources of category-to-Google-type truth: (a) `ai-verify-pipeline/index.ts` — what to STRIP, (b) `_shared/seedingCategories.ts` — what to SEED, (c) `_shared/categoryPlaceTypes.ts` — what to RETURN on-demand, (d) `mingla-admin/src/constants/categories.js` — display labels. No validator catches drift between these 4. A Google type seeded by (b) but stripped by (a) silently disappears from decks without warning. Path B in ORCH-0526 fixes this structurally (single source of truth in DB); Path A does not. Architecture-flaw + documentation-drift.

> **ORCH-0529 (NEW 2026-04-19 — race risk, S3):** `handleRunRulesFilter` has no concurrency lock. Two admin tabs running rules-filter on the same city simultaneously will both execute and write to the same place_pool rows, last writer wins. No `lock_token` field on `ai_validation_jobs`. Fix: add advisory lock by `(city_id, scope)` tuple; return 409 if held. Bundle with ORCH-0526 Phase 3 spec.

> **ORCH-0530 (NEW 2026-04-19 — historical link risk, S3):** `ai_validation_jobs.city_filter` stores city display name (e.g. "Cary"), not `city_id` UUID. If a city is renamed in `seeding_cities`, historical job-row → city lookup breaks. Add `city_id UUID FK seeding_cities` alongside the existing display string. Bundle with ORCH-0526 Phase 3 spec.

> **ORCH-0512 RETRACTED 2026-04-19:** Original framing "cost_usd=0 + completed_batches=0 regression on jobs after 2026-04-14" was a mis-attribution by the ORCH-0511 audit. Those jobs are RULES-ONLY runs which correctly produce $0 cost (no AI calls) and don't increment `completed_batches` (they don't use the AI batch loop — they paginate directly). The PRE-Apr-14 jobs were AI runs (real cost). The actual hidden flaw remaining is that `stage` is overwritten from `"rules_only"` to `"complete"` at job-end (line 1602), destroying the discriminator. The "Recent Runs" admin table also displays $0.00 cost for rules-only runs without labeling them — that's a UI labeling gap. Re-framed as: discriminator-loss + labeling-gap, both bundled into ORCH-0526 Phase 3 spec scope. ORCH-0512 closed administratively.

> **ORCH-0519 (NEW 2026-04-19 — admin error UX failure, S2):** Revoked admin (status='revoked' in `admin_users`) sees broken AIValidationPage with cryptic console errors instead of a clean "Access revoked" page. Reproducer: log into admin panel with a revoked admin account → AIValidationPage loads → `admin_ai_city_category_coverage` RPC returns HTTP 500 (RAISE 'Admin access required' propagated as 500 by PostgREST) and every `ai-verify-pipeline` edge function call returns 401/403. Root cause: every admin-gated RPC raises an exception (PostgREST converts to 500) and the edge function returns 403 (which the supabase-js SDK may surface as 401 to the browser). Constitutional #3 violation (no silent failures — errors must surface meaningfully). Discovered 2026-04-19 via user report — `sethogieva@gmail.com` is revoked, only `seth@usemingla.com` is active. Fix direction (TBD): (a) frontend wraps all admin RPCs/edge fn calls and routes 403/500-with-Admin-message to a dedicated AccessRevokedPage; (b) RPCs return JSON `{error: 'admin_revoked'}` instead of RAISE; (c) login flow checks admin_users.status before granting admin shell. S2 admin-UX. Bundle with future admin-shell hardening or address standalone.

> **ORCH-0518 (NEW 2026-04-18 — Constitutional #2 mild drift):** Two distinct AsyncStorage mechanisms track conceptually-similar "rejected" cards: `mingla_card_state_${mode}_${refreshKey}_removed` (SwipeableCards' `removedCards` Set — swipe-left rejections, mode+refreshKey-scoped) and `dismissed_cards_${user.id}_${currentMode}` (RecommendationsContext's `dismissedCards` — dismissed-sheet actions, user+mode-scoped). Different keying conventions for related concepts → "one owner per truth" drift. Not causing any observable bug today — they track different actions (swipe vs dismiss) so pair is functionally correct. Low-severity tech debt. Consolidate into a single per-context rejection store in Phase 2.5 OR a standalone cleanup sweep. Classification: architecture-flaw (minor) / documentation-drift. S3. Discovered by AH-147 forensics verification §6 OBS-2.4-3.

> **ORCH-0507 (NEW 2026-04-19 very late):** ORCH-0505 cluster extensions from second research session cross-validation. Three distinct sub-issues, all found in RecommendationsContext.tsx: (a) **generic completion-effect race at line 1346** — "Mark Fetch Complete" effect can flip `hasCompletedFetchForCurrentMode = true` BEFORE `useBoardSession.loadSession` populates `allParticipantPreferences`; this is a SECOND source of the premature-complete problem independent of CF-2.3-4 flag-gate; (b) **semantic bug in WAITING check at line 1557** — `allParticipantPrefs?.length ?? 0 < 2` conflates "data not loaded" (null → 0) with "not enough accepted participants" (actual count); should use a loading-vs-count-based distinction; (c) **dead `WAITING_FOR_PREFERENCES` state** — declared in DeckUIState union at RecommendationsContext.tsx:52, rendered at SwipeableCards.tsx:1936, never returned by the selector. > **Phase 2.3 CLOSURES (2026-04-19 late):**
> - **ORCH-0491 CLOSED:** Solo↔Collab toggle losing position. Root-cause fix: per-context DeckStateRegistry holds one DeckState per `(mode, sessionId)` tuple. Mode toggle swaps the active-context pointer — never wipes. SwipeableCards' swipe state (removedCards + currentCardIndex) is mirrored into the registry on change and restored from it on context change. Three wipe vectors all blocked under flag-on: (1) `checkAndRestoreState` modeChanged branch gated off, (2) expansion effect context-change guard early-returns before locking wrong-context IDs, (3) RESTORE effect sets `previousCardIdsSetRef = Set()` so next render INIT-branches. User device retest 2026-04-19 PASSED on DEV build.
> - **ORCH-0498 CLOSED:** Mixed-deck progressive-delivery double-wipe on solo pref change. Root-cause fix: SwipeableCards' strict-superset check detects progressive-delivery partial→final as EXPANSION (final's ID set is a superset of partial's) and suppresses wipe. User device retest confirmed mid-swipe preservation through partial→curated merge.
> - **ORCH-0493 RC#1 PARTIAL:** Collab mid-swipe wipe on incoming pref change. Superset subset closed by same expansion-signal mechanism. Non-superset case (large aggregated-prefs change producing substantively different deck) awaits Phase 2.6 which will set `isDeckExpandingWithinContext=true` on realtime pref propagation. **Do not mark fully closed until Phase 2.6 ships.**
> - **3 new invariants ESTABLISHED:** `I-PROGRESSIVE-DELIVERY-EXPANSION-NOT-REPLACEMENT` (every partial→final transition is EXPANSION — strict-superset check), `I-COLLAB-LIVE-POSITION-STABLE` (partial — Phase 2.6 completes), `I-PER-CONTEXT-DECK-STATE` (registry holds one DeckState per context; toggle swaps pointer never wipes).
> - **Ship posture:** FEATURE_FLAG_PER_CONTEXT_DECK_STATE = `__DEV__` — prod ships dark. Kill switch = flip to `false` + OTA. Coupled-exit with FEATURE_FLAG_PROGRESSIVE_DELIVERY — both flip to unconditional `true` after 1wk clean telemetry.

> **ORCH-0501 (NEW 2026-04-19):** Deck prefetch key factory at `RecommendationsContext.tsx:761-773` (inside `handleDeckCardProgress`) omits the Phase 2.3 `mode` + `sessionId` discriminants. Under FEATURE_FLAG_PER_CONTEXT_DECK_STATE=true, prefetched data lands under a mismatched key → wasted cache write, hook reads miss. Not a correctness bug (next-page fetch still works when the real boundary is crossed — just no prefetch acceleration). S3 perf/UX minor. Fix at flag-exit commit OR bundle into Phase 2.5 prefetch-persistence rework. Discovered by implementor during Phase 2.3. `implementation/IMPLEMENTATION_ORCH-0490_PHASE_2.3_PER_CONTEXT_DECK_STATE_REPORT.md §15`.
>
> **ORCH-0502 (NEW 2026-04-19):** Shared `batchSeed` provider state is NOT per-context under Phase 2.3 despite DeckStateRegistry's DeckState type having a `batchSeed` field. On context toggle (Solo↔Collab), the shared state doesn't track the new context's pagination cursor. The registry mirrors `batchSeed` but the provider's shared React state is the actual driver passed to `useDeckCards`. Subtle impact: resuming a collab session that was on batch 2 may refetch batch 0 until pagination catches up. S3. Fix at flag-exit commit OR Phase 2.5 (which reworks pagination/persistence). Discovered by implementor. `implementation/IMPLEMENTATION_ORCH-0490_PHASE_2.3_PER_CONTEXT_DECK_STATE_REPORT.md §15 #2`.

> **Phase 2.2 CLOSURES (2026-04-19):**
> - **ORCH-0485 RC#2 closed:** `deckService.fetchDeck` no longer hardcodes singles-first. `Promise.race([singlesRacer, curatedRacer])` now lets curated win when it resolves first (cold-isolate / slow-singles scenarios). `useDeckCards.onPartialReady` callback signature changed from `(cards) => void` to `(cards, {source}) => void`; cache merges via `mergeCardsByIdPreservingOrder` preserving existing positions.
> - **ORCH-0485 RC#3 closed:** Zero-singles no longer skips `onSinglesReady`. When singles settles with `value:[]`, the race path awaits curated's actual settle time (not the 20s ceiling), then fires `deliverCuratedPartial`. Zero-singles + non-empty-curated now delivers at curated's resolution time. New invariants `I-PROGRESSIVE-DELIVERY-FIRST-WIN` + `I-ZERO-SINGLES-NOT-20S-WAIT` established.
> - **ORCH-0486 closed:** mixed-deck serverPath carry-through — when singles rejects with tagged `DeckFetchError` (auth-required / pipeline-error) and curated succeeds, final return's `serverPath` carries singles' discriminant. Previously leaked `'pipeline'` default. Fix at `deckService.ts:612-618`. INV-042 + INV-043 preserved.
> - **Ship posture:** code shipped, production gated via `FEATURE_FLAG_PROGRESSIVE_DELIVERY` (defaults to `__DEV__`, so prod runs sequential-await fallback until 1-week clean telemetry). DEV builds get race path immediately. Rollback = flip constant to `false` + OTA. QA: `outputs/QA_ORCH-0490_PHASE_2.2_PROGRESSIVE_DELIVERY_REPORT.md` (0 P0/P1/P2/P3, 2 P4 doc-nits). Phase 2.3 (per-context deck state + ORCH-0498 double-wipe closure) is next.
>
> **ORCH-0494 CLOSED A (2026-04-18):** False EMPTY race eliminated via Phase 2.1. 20s safety timer + `hasStartedRef` deleted. EMPTY branch rewritten to require server verdict (`soloServerPath === 'pool-empty'` or `isDeckBatchLoaded && !deckHasMore`). `trackDeckEmptyFilter` analytic gated on `serverPath === 'pool-empty'` only (expected 60-90% event volume drop — product team notified). New invariant `I-DECK-EMPTY-IS-SERVER-VERDICT` established. QA: `outputs/QA_ORCH-0490_PHASE_2.1_DECOUPLE_LOCATION_REPORT.md` (CONDITIONAL PASS, 0 P0/P1/P2/P3).
>
> **ORCH-0485 RC#1 closed (2026-04-18):** `refreshKey` removed from `useUserLocation.ts:152` query key. Location only invalidates on location-field changes. RC#2 (singles-first hardcoded) + RC#3 (zero-singles skip) remain open for ORCH-0490 Phase 2.2.
